# TM1 TurboIntegrator Function Reference

Structured reference generated from IBM Planning Analytics TurboIntegrator function documentation.

## Format

- Each function includes category, syntax, arguments, examples, notes, and source URL.
- JSON includes structured `parameters`, `returns`, and retrieval-oriented `tags`.
- Syntax blocks are preserved as code for direct reuse in prompts or RAG pipelines.
- The `Last updated` field comes from the IBM Docs page when available.

## Functions

## ASCII and Text TurboIntegrator Functions

### ASCIIDelete

- Category: ASCII and Text TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:delete, category:ascii-text, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:file, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_tm1_ref_tifun_tifun_asciidelete.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

ASCIIDelete deletes an ASCII file.

This function is valid in TM1® TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
ASCIIDelete(FileName);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| FileName | string | The name of the ASCII file you want to delete. If a full path is not specified, TM1 searches for
the file in the server data directory. |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| FileName | The name of the ASCII file you want to delete. If a full path is not specified, TM1 searches for
the file in the server data directory. |

#### Example Notes

This example deletes the ASCII file named 2002Q1Results.cma from the
C:\exported_data
directory.

#### Examples

```ti
ASCIIDelete('C:\exported_data\2002Q1Results.cma');
```

### ASCIIOutput

- Category: ASCII and Text TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:export, category:ascii-text, feature:explicit-return, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:file, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_tm1_ref_tifun_asciioutput.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

ASCIIOutput writes a comma-delimited record to an ASCII file.

This function is valid in TM1® TurboIntegrator processes
only.

The ASCII file is opened when the first record is written, and is closed when the TurboIntegrator
procedure (Prolog, Metadata, Data, or Epilog) containing the ASCIIIOutput function finishes
processing.

Each output record generated by ASCIIOutput is limited to 64 kilobytes. If an output record
exceeds 64 kilobytes, the record is truncated and a warning is logged in the TM1ProcessError.log
file.

When ASCIIOutput encounters a String argument that pushes the output record beyond the 64
kilobyte limit, it ignores that argument and any further arguments. For example, if there are 10
String arguments and output for the first seven arguments total 65,500 bytes (just under the 64 KB
limit) while the output for the eighth argument is 50 bytes, only the output for the first seven
arguments will be written to the record, as the eighth argument causes the output to exceed the 64
kilobyte limit. If there are ten String arguments and the first argument is over 64 kilobytes, no
output is written to the record.

If you use the ASCIIOutput function to write to the same file in multiple procedures (tabs) of a
TurboIntegrator process, the file will be overwritten each time it is opened for a new
procedure.

The ASCIIOutput function generates a minor error if an error occurs while writing the ASCII file.
In addition, the function returns a value upon execution: 1 if the function successfully writes the
ASCII file and 0 on failure.

If you use ASCIIOutput to export TM1 data to an ASCII file
and then attempt to open the file in a TM1 Websheet, you will
encounter the following error.

Error occurred while converting the MS Excel workbook into XML format, hexadecimal value 0x1A is
an invalid character.

If you remove the 0x1A hexadecimal character from the Websheet, the file will open in TM1 Web.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
ASCIIOutput(FileName, String1, String2, ...Stringn);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| FileName | string | A full path to the ASCII file to which you want to write the record. Path must include a file
extension. |
| String1...String n | string | A string that corresponds to each field you want to create in the ASCII file. This argument can
be a string or a TurboIntegrator variable for a string. |

#### Returns

1 if the function successfully writes the ASCII file and 0 on failure

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| FileName | A full path to the ASCII file to which you want to write the record. Path must include a file
extension. |
| String1...String n | A string that corresponds to each field you want to create in the ASCII file. This argument can
be a string or a TurboIntegrator variable for a string. |

#### Example Notes

This example writes a record to the NewCube.cma ASCII file. Each field in the record corresponds
to a variable assigned by TurboIntegrator to a column in your data source.

#### Examples

```ti
ASCIIOutput('NewCube.cma', V1, V2, V3, V4, V5 );
```

#### Notes

- The error will be generated and the value returned only when ASCIIOutput is writing to a disk
other than the one that the server is running on. For example, if the server is running on the C:
drive and ASCIIOutput is writing to the F: drive, and the F: drive runs out of space, the error will
be trapped and the server remains alive. If the server is running on the C: drive while ASCIIOutput
is also writing to the C: drive, and that drive runs out of space, the server will terminate (as
expected).

- The ability to execute the ASCIIOutput function when the data source is a cube view is
determined by the
Allow Export as Text
capability assignment, which is set
per user group. If a user is a member of a group which is denied the ability to export data as text,
any attempt by the user to execute ASCIIOutput results in the process exiting with a permission
error. The process message log indicates
“
Execution was aborted. No security access for
ASCIIOutput.
”
For details on how the
Allow Export as Text
capability is set, see
“
Capability Assignments
”
in
TM1 Operations
.

- The ASCIIOutput function places the 0x1A hexadecimal character at the end of all generated
files. However, TM1 Web cannot open a Websheet that contains
the 0x1A hexadecimal character.

### ASCIIOutputOpen

- Category: ASCII and Text TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:export, category:ascii-text, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:file, value:number, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_tm1_ref_tifun_asciioutputopen.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

ASCIIOutputOpen appends or overwrites content in a specified existing file.

This function is valid in TurboIntegrator processes only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
ASCIIOutputOpen(FileName, OpeningMode);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| FileName | string | A full path or URL to the ASCII file to which you want to write content. The file name must
include a file extension., either .txt or .csv. |
| OpeningMode | number | A bit field flag used to configure the file opening mode. The first bit (0x1 or 0b00000001), if
set, indicates the file is opened in append mode. If not set, the existing file is opened in
overwrite mode. The second bit (0x2 or 0b00000010), if set, opens the file in FILE_SHARE_READ mode on Windows.
The second bit has no effect on Linux. FILE_OPEN_APPEND( ) and FILE_OPEN_SHARED( ) are two helper functions that can be used with
ASCIIOutputOpen. You can use them in place of the bit field flag. FILE_OPEN_APPEND( ) returns 0x1. Specify this function as the OpeningMode value to open the file
in append mode. Omit the function to open the file in overwrite mode. FILE_OPEN_SHARED( ) returns 0x2. Use this in conjunction with FILE_OPEN_APPEND( ) to open the
file in FILE_SHARE_READ mode on Windows. |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| FileName | A full path or URL to the ASCII file to which you want to write content. The file name must
include a file extension., either .txt or .csv. |
| OpeningMode | A bit field flag used to configure the file opening mode. The first bit (0x1 or 0b00000001), if
set, indicates the file is opened in append mode. If not set, the existing file is opened in
overwrite mode. The second bit (0x2 or 0b00000010), if set, opens the file in FILE_SHARE_READ mode on Windows.
The second bit has no effect on Linux. FILE_OPEN_APPEND( ) and FILE_OPEN_SHARED( ) are two helper functions that can be used with
ASCIIOutputOpen. You can use them in place of the bit field flag. FILE_OPEN_APPEND( ) returns 0x1. Specify this function as the OpeningMode value to open the file
in append mode. Omit the function to open the file in overwrite mode. FILE_OPEN_SHARED( ) returns 0x2. Use this in conjunction with FILE_OPEN_APPEND( ) to open the
file in FILE_SHARE_READ mode on Windows. |

#### Example Notes

Opens the foo.txt file in overwrite mode, without shared read access:

Opens the foo.txt file in append mode, without shared read access:

Opens the foo.txt file in overwrite mode, shared read access enabled:

Opens the foo.txt file, in append mode, shared read access enabled:

Opens the foo.txt file in append mode, shared read access enabled:

#### Examples

```ti
ASCIIOutputOpen('foo.txt', 0);
```

```ti
ASCIIOutputOpen('foo.txt', 1);
```

```ti
ASCIIOutputOpen('foo.txt', 2);
```

```ti
ASCIIOutputOpen('foo.txt', 3);
```

```ti
ASCIIOutputOpen('foo.txt', FILE_OPEN_APPEND());
```

```ti
ASCIIOutputOpen('foo.txt', FILE_OPEN_APPEND()+FILE_OPEN_SHARED());
```

### NumberToString

- Category: ASCII and Text TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: category:ascii-text, feature:locale, feature:turbointegrator-only, value:number
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_tm1_ref_tifun_numbertostring.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

NumberToString converts a number to a string, using the decimal separator for the current
user locale.

This function is valid in TM1® TurboIntegrator processes
only.

In Microsoft Windows, the decimal separator is a
Regional Options setting.

The output of this function is similar to the 'general' number format; it does not use thousands
separators and uses the minus sign (-) to denote negative numbers.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
NumberToString(Value);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Value | number | The real value that you want to convert to a string. |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Value | The real value that you want to convert to a string. |

#### Examples

```ti
nRET = NumberToString(1234.5);
```

### NumberToStringEx

- Category: ASCII and Text TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: category:ascii-text, feature:turbointegrator-only, value:number, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_tm1_ref_tifun_numbertostringex.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

NumberToStringEx converts a number to a string, using the passed string format, decimal
separator, and thousands separator.

This function is valid in TM1® TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
NumberToStringEx(Value, NumericFormat, DecimalSep, ThousandsSep);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Value | number | The real value that you want to convert to a string. |
| FormatString | string | A TM1 numeric format string that defines the format for the
function output. Numeric formats are described inIBM®
Cognos® TM1 Perspectives, TM1 Architect, and TM1 Web documentation. |
| DecimalSep | string | The decimal separator to be used in the output string. |
| ThousandsSep | string | The thousands separator to be used in the output string. |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Value | The real value that you want to convert to a string. |
| FormatString | A TM1 numeric format string that defines the format for the
function output. Numeric formats are described inIBM®
Cognos® TM1 Perspectives, TM1 Architect, and TM1 Web documentation. |
| DecimalSep | The decimal separator to be used in the output string. |
| ThousandsSep | The thousands separator to be used in the output string. |

#### Example Notes

Will return in ascii file;

7.895,23

#### Examples

```ti
sRet=NUMBERTOSTRINGEX(7895.23,'#,0.#########', ',','.');
```

```ti
ASCIIOUTPUT('number_to_string.txt',sRet);
```

### SetInputCharacterSet

- Category: ASCII and Text TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:import, category:ascii-text, feature:encoding, feature:turbointegrator-only, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_tm1_ref_tifun_setinputcharacterset.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

SetInputCharacterSet function lets you specify the character set used in a
TurboIntegrator data source.

This function is valid in TM1® TurboIntegrator processes
only.

When a TurboIntegrator process reads an external file as input, it needs to know the character
set in which that external file was written. If the file contains a valid byte-order-mark, TM1 functions will correctly convert the file to UTF-8 if
required.

For formats lacking a valid byte-order-mark, the characters must be converted from some other
encoding to UTF-8. If the proper converters are present on the machine hosting the server, the input
file will be converted to the Unicode character set required by TM1.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
SetInputCharacterSet (CharacterSet);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| CharacterSet | string | The character encoding in the input file to be used by the TurboIntegrator process. If the CharacterSet argument is not a known character type, the type defaults to the system
locale. |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| CharacterSet | The character encoding in the input file to be used by the TurboIntegrator process. If the CharacterSet argument is not a known character type, the type defaults to the system
locale. |

| Character Encoding | System Locale |
| --- | --- |
| TM1CS_ISO_8859_1 | ISO-8859-1 Latin-1, Western Europe |
| TM1CS_ISO_8859_2 | ISO-8859-2 Latin-2, Central Europe |
| TM1CS_ISO_8859_3 | ISO-8859-3 Latin-3, South Europe |
| TM1CS_ISO_8859_4 | ISO-8859-4 Latin-4, North Europe |
| TM1CS_ISO_8859_5 | ISO-8859-5 Latin/Cyrillic |
| TM1CS_ISO_8859_6 | ISO-8859-6 Latin/Arabic |
| TM1CS_ISO_8859_7 | ISO-8859-7 Latin/Greek |
| TM1CS_ISO_8859_8 | ISO-8859-8 Latin/Hebrew |
| TM1CS_ISO_8859_9 | ISO-8859-9 Latin-5, Turkish |
| TM1CS_ISO_8859_10 | ISO-8859-10 Latin-6, Nordic, |
| TM1CS_ISO_8859_11 | ISO-8859-11 Latin/Thai |
| TM1CS_ISO_8859_13 | ISO-8859-13 Latin-7, Baltic Rim |
| TM1CS_ISO_8859_14 | ISO-8859-14 Latin-8, Celtic |
| TM1CS_ISO_8859_15 | ISO-8859-15 Latin-9, replaces ISO-8859-1 |
| TM1CS_ISO_8859_16 | ISO-8859-16 Latin-10, South-Eastern Europe |
| TM1CS_WCP1250 | Microsoft
Windows Central Europe |
| TM1CS_WCP1251 | Windows Cyrillic |
| TM1CS_WCP1252 | Windows Latin-1 multilingual |
| TM1CS_WCP1253 | Windows Greek |
| TM1CS_WCP1254 | Windows Turkish |
| TM1CS_WCP1255 | Windows Hebrew |
| TM1CS_WCP1256 | Windows Arabic |
| TM1CS_WCP1257 | Windows Baltic |
| TM1CS_WCP1258 | Windows Vietnam |
| TM1CS_WCP874 | Windows Thai |
| TM1CS_WCP932 | Windows Japanese |
| TM1CS_WCP936 | Windows Simplified Chinese |
| TM1CS_WCP949 | Windows Korean |
| TM1CS_WCP950 | Windows Traditional Chinese |
| TM1CS_KOI8R | Russian and Cyrillic (KOI8-R) |
| TM1CS_GB18030 | PRC version UNICODE |
| TM1CS_BIG5 | Traditional Chinese |
| TM1CS_SHIFTJIS | JIS 0201 + JIS 0208, slightly different from CP932 |
| TM1CS_SJIS0213 | JIS 0213-2004, non-BMP required. |
| TM1CS_EUC_JP | EUC Japanese |
| TM1CS_EUC_CN | EUC Simplified Chinese |
| TM1CS_EUC_KR | EUC Korean |
| TM1CS_UTF8 | UTF-8 |
| TM1CS_UTF16 | UTF-16 Little Endian |
| TM1CS_UTF16ESC | UNICODE notation |
| TM1CS_UTF32 | UTF-32 Little Endian |
| TM1CS_OS_DEFAULT | operating system default |
| TM1CS_LOCALPATH | local encoding but UNICODE notation on non-native. |

#### Example Notes

This example specifies that the input character set for the TurboIntegrator data source is
ISO-8859-11 Latin/Thai.

#### Examples

```ti
SetInputCharacterSet ('TM1CS_ISO_8859_11');
```

### SetOutputCharacterSet

- Category: ASCII and Text TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:export, category:ascii-text, feature:encoding, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:file, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_tm1_ref_tifun_setoutputcharacterset.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

SetOutputCharacterSet lets you specify the character set to be used when writing to a
text file using TextOutput in a TurboIntegrator process.

This function is valid in TurboIntegrator processes only.

SetOutputCharacterSet should precede the TextOutput function in the process procedure (Prolog,
Metadata, Data. Epilog) where the TextOutput function appears. For example, if you want to write to
a text file using TextOutput in the Data procedure, you should first use SetOutputCharacterSet to
specify the character set in the Data procedure.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
SetOutputCharacterSet( FileName, CharacterSet );
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| FileName | string | A full path to the text file for which you want to specify a character set. The path must include
a file extension. This argument should be identical to the FileName argument for the TextOutput function. |
| CharacterSet | string | The character encoding to use when writing to the output file. For more information on the valid values for CharacterSet, see SetInputCharacterSet . |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| FileName | A full path to the text file for which you want to specify a character set. The path must include
a file extension. This argument should be identical to the FileName argument for the TextOutput function. |
| CharacterSet | The character encoding to use when writing to the output file. For more information on the valid values for CharacterSet, see SetInputCharacterSet . |

### SetOutputEscapeDoubleQuote

- Category: ASCII and Text TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:export, category:ascii-text, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:file, value:number, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_tm1_ref_tifun_setoutputescapedoublequote.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

SetOutputEscapeDoubleQuote allows you to escape double quotes that appear in element
names or data values when exporting a cube view to a .csv file.

This function is valid in TM1® TurboIntegrator processes
only.

When SetOutputEscapeDoubleQuote is included in your TurboIntegrator script and set to 1, the
exported file retains the double quote positions as they appear in your source cube view by escaping
each double quote within another pair of double quotes. For example, if an element in your source
view is named "Region", the element is exported as """Region""" in the .csv output file.

When SetOutputEscapeDoubleQuote is
not
included in your TurboIntegrator script or is set
to 0, the exported file does not escape any double quotes that appear in your source cube.

SetOutputEscapeDoubleQuote is used in conjunction with the ASCIIOutput function, which is the
function that actually writes the output file. SetOutputEscapeDoubleQuote should precede ASCIIOutput
in your TurboIntegrator script, and both functions should use the same FileName parameter value.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
SetOutputEscapeDoubleQuote(FileName, Num);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| FileName | string | A full path to the file to which you want to write the cube view. Path must include a file
extension. |
| Num | number | A flag that determines if double quotes are escaped in the output file. 1 indicates that double quotes will be escaped in the output file. 0 indicates that double quotes will not be escaped in the output file. |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| FileName | A full path to the file to which you want to write the cube view. Path must include a file
extension. |
| Num | A flag that determines if double quotes are escaped in the output file. 1 indicates that double quotes will be escaped in the output file. 0 indicates that double quotes will not be escaped in the output file. |

#### Example Notes

This example escapes any double quotes encountered in the source cube view when writing output to
the C:\temp\cube1.csv file.

#### Examples

```ti
SetOutputEscapeDoubleQuote('C:\temp\cube1.csv', 1);
```

### StringToNumber

- Category: ASCII and Text TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: category:ascii-text, feature:locale, feature:turbointegrator-only, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_tm1_ref_tifun_stringtonumber.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

StringToNumber converts a string to a number, using the decimal separator for the current
user locale. If the input string is an invalid number string, the value returned will be an invalid
floating point value. In Microsoft Windows, the decimal
separator is a Regional Options setting.

This function is valid in TM1® TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
StringToNumber(String);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| String | string | The string you want to convert to a number. |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| String | The string you want to convert to a number. |

#### Examples

```ti
nRET = StringToNumber('123.45');
```

### StringToNumberEx

- Category: ASCII and Text TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: category:ascii-text, feature:turbointegrator-only, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_tm1_ref_tifun_stringtonumberex.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

StringToNumberEx converts a string to a number, using the passed decimal separator and
thousands separator. If the input string is an invalid number string, the value returned will be an
invalid floating point value.

This function is valid in TM1® TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
StringToNumberEx(String, DecimalSep, ThousandsSep);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| String | string | The string that you want to convert to a number. |
| DecimalSep | string | The decimal separator to be used in the output number. |
| ThousandsSep | string | The thousands separator to be used in the output number. |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| String | The string that you want to convert to a number. |
| DecimalSep | The decimal separator to be used in the output number. |
| ThousandsSep | The thousands separator to be used in the output number. |

#### Examples

```ti
nRET = StringToNumberEx('12453.45', ' . ', ' , ');
```

### TextOutput

- Category: ASCII and Text TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:export, category:ascii-text, feature:encoding, feature:explicit-return, feature:locale, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:file, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_tm1_ref_tifun_textoutput.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

TextOutput writes a comma-delimited record to a text file.

This function is valid in TM1® TurboIntegrator processes
only.

By default TextOutput writes characters in the locale character set of the server machine. To
create a file in a different character set, call the function
SetOutputCharacterSet
before calling TextOutput.

The text file is opened when the first record is written, and is closed when the TurboIntegrator
procedure (Prolog, Metadata, Data, or Epilog) containing the TextOutput function finishes
processing.

If you use the TextOutput function to write to the same file in multiple procedures (tabs) of a
TurboIntegrator process, the file will be overwritten each time it is opened for a new
procedure.

Each output record generated by TextOutput is limited to 8000 bytes. If an output record exceeds
8000 bytes, the record is truncated and a warning is logged in the TM1ProcessError.log file.

When TextOutput encounters a String argument that pushes the output record beyond the 8000 byte
limit, it ignores that argument and any further arguments. For example, if there are 10 String
arguments and output for the first seven arguments total 7950 bytes while the output for the eighth
argument is 51 bytes, only the output for the first seven arguments will be written to the record.
If there are ten String arguments and the first argument is over 8000 bytes, no output will be
written to the record.

The TextOutput function generates a minor error if an error occurs while writing the text file.
In addition, the function returns a value upon execution: 1 if the function successfully writes the
text file and 0 on failure.

The error will be generated and the value returned only when TextOutput is writing to a disk
other than the one that the server is running on. For example, if the server is running on the C:
drive and TextOutput is writing to the F: drive, and the F: drive runs out of space, the error will
be trapped and the server remains alive. If the server is running on the C: drive while TextOutput
is also writing to the C: drive, and that drive runs out of space, the server will terminate (as
expected).

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
TextOutput(FileName, String1, String2, ...Stringn);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| FileName | string | A full path to the text file to which you want to write the record. Path must include a file
extension. |
| String1...String n | string | A string that corresponds to each field you want to create in the text file. This argument can be
a string or a TurboIntegrator variable for a string. |

#### Returns

1 if the function successfully writes the text file and 0 on failure

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| FileName | A full path to the text file to which you want to write the record. Path must include a file
extension. |
| String1...String n | A string that corresponds to each field you want to create in the text file. This argument can be
a string or a TurboIntegrator variable for a string. |

#### Example Notes

This example writes a record to the NewCube.cma file. Each field in the record corresponds to a
variable assigned by TurboIntegrator to a column in your data source.

#### Examples

```ti
TextOutput('NewCube.cma', V1, V2, V3, V4, V5 );
```

#### Notes

- The ability to execute the TextOutput function when the data source is a cube view is
determined by the
Allow Export as Text
capability assignment, which is set
per user group. If a user is a member of a group which is denied the ability to export data as text,
any attempt by the user to execute TextOutput results in the process exiting with a permission
error. The process message log indicates
“
Execution was aborted. No security access for
TextOutput.
”
For details on how the
Allow Export as Text
capability is set, see
“
Capability Assignments
”
in the
IBM Cognos TM1 Operations
documentation.

### TurboIntegrator Functions

- Category: ASCII and Text TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: category:ascii-text
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/c_tm1turbointegratorfunctions_n70006.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

TurboIntegrator lets you manipulate
Planning Analytics
data and metadata when you define a
process.

This is accomplished through the use of functions in the Prolog, Metadata, Data, and Epilog
sub-tabs within the Advanced tab of the TurboIntegrator window. These sub-tabs include generated
statements based on settings and options you select when defining a TurboIntegrator process. Any
functions you create must appear after the generated statements. For details on creating processes
with TurboIntegrator, see the
TurboIntegrator
documentation.

- Valid in: unknown

## Attribute Manipulation TurboIntegrator Functions

### AttrDelete

- Category: Attribute Manipulation TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:delete, category:attribute, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:attribute, object:dimension, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_tm1_ref_tifun_attrdelete.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

AttrDelete deletes an element attribute from the TM1® database.

This function is valid in TM1 TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
AttrDelete(DimName, AttrName);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DimName | string | The dimension for which you want to delete an element attribute. |
| AttrName | string | The name of the attribute you want to delete. |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| DimName | The dimension for which you want to delete an element attribute. |
| AttrName | The name of the attribute you want to delete. |

#### Example Notes

This example deletes the InteriorColor element attribute for the Model dimension.

#### Examples

```ti
AttrDelete('Model', 'InteriorColor');
```

### AttrInsert

- Category: Attribute Manipulation TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:create, category:attribute, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:attribute, object:dimension, value:enum, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_tm1_ref_tifun_attrinsert.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

AttrInsert creates a new element attribute for a dimension. The function can create a
string, numeric, or alias attribute.

This function is valid in TM1® TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
AttrInsert(DimName, PrevAttr, AttrName, Type);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DimName | string | The dimension for which you want to create an element attribute. |
| PrevAttr | string | The attribute that precedes the attribute you are creating. |
| AttrName | string | The name you want to assign to the new attribute. |
| Type | enum | The type of attribute. There are three possible values for the Type argument: N - Creates a numeric attribute. S - Creates a string attribute. A - Creates an alias attribute. |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| DimName | The dimension for which you want to create an element attribute. |
| PrevAttr | The attribute that precedes the attribute you are creating. |
| AttrName | The name you want to assign to the new attribute. |
| Type | The type of attribute. There are three possible values for the Type argument: N - Creates a numeric attribute. S - Creates a string attribute. A - Creates an alias attribute. |

#### Example Notes

This example creates the InteriorColor string attribute for the Model dimension. This attribute
is inserted after the Transmission attribute.

#### Examples

```ti
AttrInsert('Model', 'Transmission', 'InteriorColor','S');
```

### ATTRNL

- Category: Attribute Manipulation TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:read, category:attribute, feature:locale, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:attribute, object:dimension, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/t_ref_ti_func_attrnl.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

ATTRNL returns a numeric attribute for a specified element of a dimension.

This function is valid in TM1® TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
ATTRNL(DimName, ElName, AttrName, [LangLocaleCode]);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DimName | string | A valid dimension name. |
| ElName | string | An element of the dimension. |
| AttrName | string | The attribute for which you want to retrieve a value. This argument must be a valid attribute of
the element. |
| LangLocaleCode | string | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code for which you want to return a value. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the international language codes listed in the
}Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the user's current locale is used as the
LangLocaleCode argument. If an attribute value does not exist for the LangLocaleCode, the value for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode is returned. If an attribute value does not exist for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode, the base attribute value is returned. For example if the LangLocaleCode is fr-CA , the function returns the attribute
value for the fr-CA locale if available. If the attribute value for fr-CA is not available, the function attempts to return the attribute value for the
parent fr locale. If the attribute value for fr is not available,
the base attribute value is returned |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| DimName | A valid dimension name. |
| ElName | An element of the dimension. |
| AttrName | The attribute for which you want to retrieve a value. This argument must be a valid attribute of
the element. |
| LangLocaleCode | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code for which you want to return a value. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the international language codes listed in the
}Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the user's current locale is used as the
LangLocaleCode argument. If an attribute value does not exist for the LangLocaleCode, the value for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode is returned. If an attribute value does not exist for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode, the base attribute value is returned. For example if the LangLocaleCode is fr-CA , the function returns the attribute
value for the fr-CA locale if available. If the attribute value for fr-CA is not available, the function attempts to return the attribute value for the
parent fr locale. If the attribute value for fr is not available,
the base attribute value is returned |

#### Example Notes

In this example, the function returns the numeric value of the Engine Size attribute of the L
Series 1.8L Sedan element in the Model dimension for the French locale.

#### Examples

```ti
ATTRNL('Model', 'L Series 1.8L Sedan', 'Engine Size', 'fr');
```

### AttrPutN

- Category: Attribute Manipulation TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:update, category:attribute, feature:locale, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:attribute, object:dimension, value:number, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_tm1_ref_tifun_attrputn.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

AttrPutN assigns a value to a numeric element attribute.

This function is valid in TM1® TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
AttrPutN( Value, DimName, ElName, AttrName, [LangLocaleCode] );
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Value | number | The numeric value you want to assign to an element attribute. |
| DimName | string | The parent dimension of the element for which you want to assign an attribute value. |
| ElName | string | The element for which you want to assign an attribute value. |
| AttrName | string | The attribute whose value you want to assign. |
| LangLocaleCode | string | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code to which the NumericValue applies. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the ISO 639-1 international language codes listed in
the }Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the base attribute value is updated. |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Value | The numeric value you want to assign to an element attribute. |
| DimName | The parent dimension of the element for which you want to assign an attribute value. |
| ElName | The element for which you want to assign an attribute value. |
| AttrName | The attribute whose value you want to assign. |
| LangLocaleCode | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code to which the NumericValue applies. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the ISO 639-1 international language codes listed in
the }Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the base attribute value is updated. |

#### Example Notes

This example assigns the value 2257993 to the ProdCode attribute of the S Series 1.8L Sedan in
the Model dimension.

#### Examples

```ti
AttrPutN(2257993, 'Model', ' S Series 1.8L Sedan ','ProdCode');
```

### ChoreAttrInsert

- Category: Attribute Manipulation TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:create, category:attribute, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:attribute, object:chore, value:enum, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_ti_func_choreattrinsert.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

ChoreAttrInsert creates a new attribute for chores on your TM1® server. The function can create a string, numeric, or alias attribute.

This function is valid in TM1 TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
ChoreAttrInsert( PrevAttrName, NewAttrName, AttrType);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| PrevAttrName | string | The attribute that precedes the attribute you are creating. If there is no previous attribute or
you want the new attribute to be the first attribute for chores, leave this argument empty. |
| NewAttrName | string | The name you want to assign to the new chore attribute. |
| AttrType | enum | The type of attribute. There are three possible values for the AttrType argument: N - Creates a numeric attribute. S - Creates a string attribute. A - Creates an alias attribute. |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| PrevAttrName | The attribute that precedes the attribute you are creating. If there is no previous attribute or
you want the new attribute to be the first attribute for chores, leave this argument empty. |
| NewAttrName | The name you want to assign to the new chore attribute. |
| AttrType | The type of attribute. There are three possible values for the AttrType argument: N - Creates a numeric attribute. S - Creates a string attribute. A - Creates an alias attribute. |

#### Example Notes

This example creates the Description string attribute for chores. This attribute is inserted
after the Owner attribute.

#### Examples

```ti
ChoreAttrInsert('Owner', 'Description', 'S');
```

#### Notes

- If you update an existing chore attribute, you must first delete the existing attribute using
the function ChoreAttrDelete. You can then use ChoreAttrInsert to recreate the attribute with your
desired changes. If you attempt to update an existing attribute without first deleting it, the
insert fails without a warning or error. The existing attribute remains unchanged; it is neither
updated nor overwritten.

### ChoreAttrN

### ChoreAttrNL

- Category: Attribute Manipulation TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:read, category:attribute, feature:locale, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:attribute, object:chore, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_ti_func_choreattrnl.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

ChoreAttrNL returns an attribute's numeric value for a specified chore with respect to a
given locale.

This function is valid in TM1® TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
ChoreAttrNL(ChoreName, AttrName, [LangLocaleCode]);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ChoreName | string | A valid chore name. |
| AttrName | string | The attribute for which you want to retrieve a value. This argument must be a valid attribute of
the chore. |
| LangLocaleCode | string | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code for which you want to return a value. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the international language codes listed in the
}Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the user's current locale is used as the
LangLocaleCode argument. If an attribute value does not exist for the LangLocaleCode, the value for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode is returned. If an attribute value does not exist for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode, the base attribute value is returned. For example if the LangLocaleCode is fr-CA , the function returns the attribute
value for the fr-CA (French-Canada) locale if available. If the attribute value for fr-CA is not available, the function attempts to return the attribute value for the
parent fr (French) locale. If the attribute value for fr is not
available, the base attribute value is returned |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| ChoreName | A valid chore name. |
| AttrName | The attribute for which you want to retrieve a value. This argument must be a valid attribute of
the chore. |
| LangLocaleCode | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code for which you want to return a value. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the international language codes listed in the
}Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the user's current locale is used as the
LangLocaleCode argument. If an attribute value does not exist for the LangLocaleCode, the value for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode is returned. If an attribute value does not exist for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode, the base attribute value is returned. For example if the LangLocaleCode is fr-CA , the function returns the attribute
value for the fr-CA (French-Canada) locale if available. If the attribute value for fr-CA is not available, the function attempts to return the attribute value for the
parent fr (French) locale. If the attribute value for fr is not
available, the base attribute value is returned |

#### Example Notes

In this example, the function returns the numeric value of the Division_Code attribute of the
Import chore for the French locale.

#### Examples

```ti
ChoreAttrNL('Import', 'Division_Code', 'fr');
```

This example assigns the string value Ricci to the Owner attribute of the Import chore, for the
French language locale code.

#### Examples

```ti
ChoreAttrPutS('Ricci', 'Import', 'Owner', 'fr');
```

### ChoreAttrSL

- Category: Attribute Manipulation TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:read, category:attribute, feature:locale, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:attribute, object:chore, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_ti_func_choreattrsl.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

ChoreAttrSL returns a string attribute value for a specified chore with respect to a
given locale.

This function is valid in TM1® TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
ChoreAttrSL(ChoreName, AttrName, [LangLocaleCode]);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ChoreName | string | A valid chore name. |
| AttrName | string | The attribute for which you want to retrieve a value. This argument must be a valid attribute of
the chore. |
| LangLocaleCode | string | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code for which you want to return a value. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the international language codes listed in the
}Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the user's current locale is used as the
LangLocaleCode argument. If an attribute value does not exist for the LangLocaleCode, the value for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode is returned. If an attribute value does not exist for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode, the base attribute value is returned. For example if the LangLocaleCode is fr-CA , the function returns the attribute
value for the fr-CA (French-Canada) locale if available. If the attribute value for fr-CA is not available, the function attempts to return the attribute value for the
parent fr (French) locale. If the attribute value for fr is not
available, the base attribute value is returned |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| ChoreName | A valid chore name. |
| AttrName | The attribute for which you want to retrieve a value. This argument must be a valid attribute of
the chore. |
| LangLocaleCode | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code for which you want to return a value. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the international language codes listed in the
}Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the user's current locale is used as the
LangLocaleCode argument. If an attribute value does not exist for the LangLocaleCode, the value for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode is returned. If an attribute value does not exist for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode, the base attribute value is returned. For example if the LangLocaleCode is fr-CA , the function returns the attribute
value for the fr-CA (French-Canada) locale if available. If the attribute value for fr-CA is not available, the function attempts to return the attribute value for the
parent fr (French) locale. If the attribute value for fr is not
available, the base attribute value is returned |

#### Example Notes

In this example, the function returns the string value of the Owner attribute of the
Depreciate_Inventory chore for the French locale.

#### Examples

```ti
ChoreAttrSL('Depreciate_Inventory', 'Owner', 'fr');
```

### CubeAttrInsert

- Category: Attribute Manipulation TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:create, category:attribute, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:attribute, object:cube, value:enum, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_ti_func_cubeattrinsert.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

CubeAttrInsert creates a new attribute for cubes on your TM1® server. The function can create a string, numeric, or alias attribute.

This function is valid in TM1 TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
CubeAttrInsert( PrevAttrName, NewAttrName, AttrType);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| PrevAttrName | string | The attribute that precedes the attribute you are creating. If there is no previous attribute or
you want the new attribute to be the first attribute for cubes, leave this argument empty. |
| NewAttrName | string | The name you want to assign to the new cube attribute. |
| AttrType | enum | The type of attribute. There are three possible values for the AttrType argument: N - Creates a numeric attribute. S - Creates a string attribute. A - Creates an alias attribute. |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| PrevAttrName | The attribute that precedes the attribute you are creating. If there is no previous attribute or
you want the new attribute to be the first attribute for cubes, leave this argument empty. |
| NewAttrName | The name you want to assign to the new cube attribute. |
| AttrType | The type of attribute. There are three possible values for the AttrType argument: N - Creates a numeric attribute. S - Creates a string attribute. A - Creates an alias attribute. |

#### Example Notes

This example creates the Description string attribute for cubes. This attribute is inserted after
the Owner attribute.

#### Examples

```ti
CubeAttrInsert('Owner', 'Description', 'S');
```

#### Notes

- If you update an existing cube attribute, you must first delete the existing attribute using
the function CubeAttrDelete. You can then use CubeAttrInsert to recreate the attribute with your
desired changes. If you attempt to update an existing attribute without first deleting it, the
insert fails without a warning or error. The existing attribute remains unchanged; it is neither
updated nor overwritten.

### CubeAttrPutN

- Category: Attribute Manipulation TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:update, category:attribute, feature:locale, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:attribute, object:cube, value:number, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_ti_func_cubeattrputn.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

CubeAttrPutN assigns a value to a numeric cube attribute.

This function is valid in TM1® TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
CubeAttrPutN(NumericValue, CubeName, AttrName, [LangLocaleCode] );
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| NumericValue | number | The value you want to assign to a cube attribute. |
| CubeName | string | The cube for which you want to assign an attribute value. |
| AttrName | string | The attribute whose value you want to assign. |
| LangLocaleCode | string | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code to which the NumericValue applies. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the ISO 639-1 international language codes listed in
the }Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the base attribute value is updated. |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NumericValue | The value you want to assign to a cube attribute. |
| CubeName | The cube for which you want to assign an attribute value. |
| AttrName | The attribute whose value you want to assign. |
| LangLocaleCode | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code to which the NumericValue applies. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the ISO 639-1 international language codes listed in
the }Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the base attribute value is updated. |

#### Example Notes

This example assigns the value 07161994 to the AccountingCode attribute of the Sales cube for the
French language locale code.

#### Examples

```ti
CubeAttrPutN(07161994, 'Sales', 'AccountingCode','fr');
```

### DimensionAttrInsert

- Category: Attribute Manipulation TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:create, category:attribute, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:attribute, object:dimension, value:enum, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_ti_func_dimensionattrinsert.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

DimensionAttrInsert creates a new attribute for dimensions on your TM1® server. The function can create a string, numeric, or alias attribute.

This function is valid in TM1 TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
DimensionAttrInsert( PrevAttrName, NewAttrName, AttrType);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| PrevAttrName | string | The attribute that precedes the attribute you are creating. If there is no previous attribute or
you want the new attribute to be the first attribute for dimensions, leave this argument empty. |
| NewAttrName | string | The name you want to assign to the new dimension attribute. |
| AttrType | enum | The type of attribute. There are three possible values for the AttrType argument: N - Creates a numeric attribute. S - Creates a string attribute. A - Creates an alias attribute. |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| PrevAttrName | The attribute that precedes the attribute you are creating. If there is no previous attribute or
you want the new attribute to be the first attribute for dimensions, leave this argument empty. |
| NewAttrName | The name you want to assign to the new dimension attribute. |
| AttrType | The type of attribute. There are three possible values for the AttrType argument: N - Creates a numeric attribute. S - Creates a string attribute. A - Creates an alias attribute. |

#### Example Notes

This example creates the Description string attribute for dimensions. Because there is no
PrevAttrName parameter, this attribute is inserted as the first attribute for dimensions on your TM1 server.

#### Examples

```ti
DimensionAttrInsert('', 'Description', 'S');
```

#### Notes

- If you update an existing dimension attribute, you must first delete the existing attribute
using the function DimensionAttrDelete. You can then use DimensionAttrInsert to recreate the
attribute with your desired changes.  If you attempt to update an existing attribute without first
deleting it, the insert fails without a warning or error. The existing attribute remains unchanged;
it is neither updated nor overwritten.

the }Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the base attribute value is updated. |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| String | The string you want to assign to a dimension attribute. |
| DimensionName | The dimension for which you want to assign an attribute value. |
| AttrName | The attribute whose value you want to assign. |
| LangLocaleCode | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code to which the NumericValue applies. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the ISO 639-1 international language codes listed in
the }Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the base attribute value is updated. |

#### Example Notes

This example assigns the string value Prototype to the Description attribute of the Model
dimension for the French language locale code.

#### Examples

```ti
DimensionAttrPutS('Prototype', 'Model', 'Description','fr');
```

### DimensionATTRSL

- Category: Attribute Manipulation TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:read, category:attribute, feature:locale, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:attribute, object:dimension, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_tm1_ti_func_dimensionattrnsl.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

DimensionATTRSL returns a string attribute value for a specified dimension with respect
to a given locale.

This function is valid in TM1® TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
DimensionATTRSL(DimName, AttrName, [LangLocaleCode]);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DimName | string | A valid dimension name. |
| AttrName | string | The attribute for which you want to retrieve a value. This argument must be a valid attribute of
the dimension. |
| LangLocaleCode | string | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code for which you want to return a value. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the international language codes listed in the
}Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the user's current locale is used as the
LangLocaleCode argument. If an attribute value does not exist for the LangLocaleCode, the value for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode is returned. If an attribute value does not exist for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode, the base attribute value is returned. For example if the LangLocaleCode is fr-CA , the function returns the attribute
value for the fr-CA (French-Canada) locale if available. If the attribute value for fr-CA is not available, the function attempts to return the attribute value for the
parent fr (French) locale. If the attribute value for fr is not
available, the base attribute value is returned |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| DimName | A valid dimension name. |
| AttrName | The attribute for which you want to retrieve a value. This argument must be a valid attribute of
the dimension. |
| LangLocaleCode | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code for which you want to return a value. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the international language codes listed in the
}Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the user's current locale is used as the
LangLocaleCode argument. If an attribute value does not exist for the LangLocaleCode, the value for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode is returned. If an attribute value does not exist for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode, the base attribute value is returned. For example if the LangLocaleCode is fr-CA , the function returns the attribute
value for the fr-CA (French-Canada) locale if available. If the attribute value for fr-CA is not available, the function attempts to return the attribute value for the
parent fr (French) locale. If the attribute value for fr is not
available, the base attribute value is returned |

#### Example Notes

In this example, the function returns the string value of the Manager attribute of the
Plan_Business_Unit dimension for the French locale.

#### Examples

```ti
DimensionATTRSL('Plan_Business_Unit', 'Manager', 'fr');
```

### ElementAttrInsert

- Category: Attribute Manipulation TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:create, category:attribute, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:attribute, object:dimension, object:hierarchy, value:enum, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_tm1_ref_tifun_elementattrinsert.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

ElementAttrInsert creates a new element attribute for a dimension. The function can
create a string, numeric, or alias attribute.

This function is valid in TM1® TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
ElementAttrInsert(DimName, HierName, PrevAttr, AttrName, Type);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DimName | string | The dimension for which you want to create an element attribute. |
| HierName | string | The name of the hierarchy within the dimension. |
| PrevAttr | string | The attribute that precedes the attribute you are creating. |
| AttrName | string | The name you want to assign to the new attribute. |
| Type | enum | The type of attribute. There are three possible values for the Type argument: N - Creates a numeric attribute. S - Creates a string attribute. A - Creates an alias attribute. |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| DimName | The dimension for which you want to create an element attribute. |
| HierName | The name of the hierarchy within the dimension. |
| PrevAttr | The attribute that precedes the attribute you are creating. |
| AttrName | The name you want to assign to the new attribute. |
| Type | The type of attribute. There are three possible values for the Type argument: N - Creates a numeric attribute. S - Creates a string attribute. A - Creates an alias attribute. |

#### Example Notes

This example creates the InteriorColor string attribute in the Automobile hierarchy in the Model
dimension. This attribute is inserted after the Transmission attribute.

#### Examples

```ti
ElementAttrInsert('Model', 'Automobile', 'Transmission', 'InteriorColor','S');
```

### ElementATTRNL

- Category: Attribute Manipulation TurboIntegrator Functions

only.

```ti

```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DimName | string | A valid dimension name. |
| HierName | string | The name of the hierarchy within the dimension. |
| ElName | string | An element of the dimension. |
| AttrName | string | The attribute for which you want to retrieve a value. This argument must be a valid attribute of
the element. |
| LangLocaleCode | string | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code for which you want to return a value. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the international language codes listed in the
}Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the user's current locale is used as the
LangLocaleCode argument. If an attribute value does not exist for the LangLocaleCode, the value for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode is returned. If an attribute value does not exist for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode, the base attribute value is returned. For example if the LangLocaleCode is fr-CA , the function returns the attribute
value for the fr-CA locale if available. If the attribute value for fr-CA is not available, the function attempts to return the attribute value for the
parent fr locale. If the attribute value for fr is not available,
the base attribute value is returned |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| DimName | A valid dimension name. |
| HierName | The name of the hierarchy within the dimension. |
| ElName | An element of the dimension. |
| AttrName | The attribute for which you want to retrieve a value. This argument must be a valid attribute of
the element. |
| LangLocaleCode | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code for which you want to return a value. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the international language codes listed in the
}Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the user's current locale is used as the
LangLocaleCode argument. If an attribute value does not exist for the LangLocaleCode, the value for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode is returned. If an attribute value does not exist for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode, the base attribute value is returned. For example if the LangLocaleCode is fr-CA , the function returns the attribute
value for the fr-CA locale if available. If the attribute value for fr-CA is not available, the function attempts to return the attribute value for the
parent fr locale. If the attribute value for fr is not available,
the base attribute value is returned |


| AttrName | The attribute whose value you want to assign. |

the }Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the base attribute value is updated. |

#### Example Notes

This example assigns the string value Prototype to the Description attribute of the Model
dimension for the French language locale code. This change is applied to the Receivables hierarchy
in the Model dimension.

#### Examples

```ti
HierarchyAttrPutS('Prototype', 'Model', 'Receivables', 'Description','fr');
```

### HierarchyATTRS

- Category: Attribute Manipulation TurboIntegrator Functions

### HierarchyATTRSL

- Category: Attribute Manipulation TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:read, category:attribute, feature:locale, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:attribute, object:dimension, object:hierarchy, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_tm1_ti_func_hierarchyattrsl.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

HierarchyATTRSL returns a string attribute value for a specified hierarchy within a
dimension with respect to a given locale.

This function is valid in TM1® TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
HierarchyATTRSL(DimName, HierName, AttrName, [LangLocaleCode]);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DimName | string | A valid dimension name. |
| HierName | string | The name of the hierarchy within the dimension. |
| AttrName | string | The attribute for which you want to retrieve a value. This argument must be a valid attribute of
the dimension. |
| LangLocaleCode | string | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code for which you want to return a value. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the international language codes listed in the
}Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the user's current locale is used as the
LangLocaleCode argument. If an attribute value does not exist for the LangLocaleCode, the value for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode is returned. If an attribute value does not exist for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode, the base attribute value is returned. For example if the LangLocaleCode is fr-CA , the function returns the attribute
value for the fr-CA (French-Canada) locale if available. If the attribute value for fr-CA is not available, the function attempts to return the attribute value for the
parent fr (French) locale. If the attribute value for fr is not
available, the base attribute value is returned |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| DimName | A valid dimension name. |
| HierName | The name of the hierarchy within the dimension. |
| AttrName | The attribute for which you want to retrieve a value. This argument must be a valid attribute of
the dimension. |
| LangLocaleCode | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code for which you want to return a value. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the international language codes listed in the
}Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the user's current locale is used as the
LangLocaleCode argument. If an attribute value does not exist for the LangLocaleCode, the value for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode is returned. If an attribute value does not exist for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode, the base attribute value is returned. For example if the LangLocaleCode is fr-CA , the function returns the attribute
value for the fr-CA (French-Canada) locale if available. If the attribute value for fr-CA is not available, the function attempts to return the attribute value for the
parent fr (French) locale. If the attribute value for fr is not
available, the base attribute value is returned |

#### Example Notes

In this example, the function returns the string value of the Manager attribute of the
Plan_Business_Unit dimension for the French locale. This function applies to the Equipment
hierarchy.

#### Examples

```ti
HierarchyATTRSL('Plan_Business_Unit', 'Equipment', 'Manager', 'fr');
```

### HierarchySubsetAttrInsert

- Category: Attribute Manipulation TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:create, category:attribute, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:attribute, object:dimension, object:hierarchy, object:subset, value:enum, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_ti_func_hierarchysubsetattrinsert.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

HierarchySubsetAttrInsert creates a new attribute for subsets on your TM1® server. The function creates a string, numeric, or alias attribute.

This function is valid in TM1 TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
HierarchySubsetAttrInsert( Dimension, Hierarchy, PrevAttrName, NewAttrName, AttrType);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Dimension | string | The name of the dimension whose subsets are being updated. |
| Hierarchy | string | The name of a hierarchy in a dimension. |
| PrevAttrName | string | The attribute that precedes the attribute you are creating. If there is no previous attribute or
you want the new attribute to be the first attribute for subsets, leave this argument empty. |
| NewAttrName | string | The name you want to assign to the new subset attribute. |
| AttrType | enum | The type of attribute. There are three possible values for the AttrType argument: N - Creates a numeric attribute. S - Creates a string attribute. A - Creates an alias attribute. |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Dimension | The name of the dimension whose subsets are being updated. |
| Hierarchy | The name of a hierarchy in a dimension. |
| PrevAttrName | The attribute that precedes the attribute you are creating. If there is no previous attribute or
you want the new attribute to be the first attribute for subsets, leave this argument empty. |
| NewAttrName | The name you want to assign to the new subset attribute. |
| AttrType | The type of attribute. There are three possible values for the AttrType argument: N - Creates a numeric attribute. S - Creates a string attribute. A - Creates an alias attribute. |

#### Example Notes

This example creates the Description string attribute for subsets in the Z hierarchy of the Model
dimension. Because there is no PrevAttrName parameter, this attribute is inserted as the first
attribute for subsets on your TM1 server.

#### Examples

```ti
HierarchySubsetAttrInsert('Model', 'Z', '', 'Description', 'S');
```

#### Notes

- If you update an existing subset attribute, you must first delete the existing attribute using
the function HierarchySubsetAttrDelete. You can then use HierarchySubsetAttrInsert to recreate the
attribute with your desired changes. If you attempt to update an existing attribute without first
deleting it, the insert fails without a warning or error. The existing attribute remains unchanged;
it is neither updated nor overwritten.

### ProcessAttrInsert

- Category: Attribute Manipulation TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:create, category:attribute, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:attribute, value:enum, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_ti_func_processattrinsert.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

ProcessAttrInsert creates a new attribute for processes on your TM1® server. The function can create a string, numeric, or alias attribute.

This function is valid in TM1 TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
ProcessAttrInsert( PrevAttrName, NewAttrName, AttrType);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| PrevAttrName | string | The attribute that precedes the attribute you are creating. If there is no previous attribute or
you want the new attribute to be the first attribute for processes, leave this argument empty. |
| NewAttrName | string | The name you want to assign to the new process attribute. |
| AttrType | enum | The type of attribute. There are three possible values for the AttrType argument: N - Creates a numeric attribute. S - Creates a string attribute. A - Creates an alias attribute. |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| PrevAttrName | The attribute that precedes the attribute you are creating. If there is no previous attribute or
you want the new attribute to be the first attribute for processes, leave this argument empty. |
| NewAttrName | The name you want to assign to the new process attribute. |
| AttrType | The type of attribute. There are three possible values for the AttrType argument: N - Creates a numeric attribute. S - Creates a string attribute. A - Creates an alias attribute. |

#### Example Notes

This example creates the Description string attribute for processes. This attribute is inserted
after the Owner attribute.

#### Examples

```ti
ProcessAttrInsert('Owner', 'Description', 'S');
```

#### Notes

- If you update an existing process attribute, you must first delete the existing attribute
using the function ProcessAttrDelete. You can then use ProcessAttrInsert to recreate the attribute
with your desired changes. If you attempt to update an existing attribute without first deleting it,
the insert fails without a warning or error. The existing attribute remains unchanged; it is neither
updated nor overwritten.

### ProcessAttrN

| --- | --- |

| AttrName | The attribute for which you want to retrieve a value. This argument must be a valid attribute of

### ProcessAttrNL

- Category: Attribute Manipulation TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:read, category:attribute, feature:locale, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:attribute, object:process, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_ti_func_processattrnl.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

ProcessAttrNL returns an attribute's numeric value for a specified process with respect
to a given locale.

This function is valid in TM1® TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
ProcessAttrNL(ProcessName, AttrName, [LangLocaleCode]);
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ProcessName | string | A valid process name. |
| AttrName | string | The attribute for which you want to retrieve a value. This argument must be a valid attribute of
the process. |
| LangLocaleCode | string | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code for which you want to return a value. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the international language codes listed in the
}Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the user's current locale is used as the
LangLocaleCode argument. If an attribute value does not exist for the LangLocaleCode, the value for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode is returned. If an attribute value does not exist for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode, the base attribute value is returned. For example if the LangLocaleCode is fr-CA , the function returns the attribute
value for the fr-CA (French-Canada) locale if available. If the attribute value for fr-CA is not available, the function attempts to return the attribute value for the
parent fr (French) locale. If the attribute value for fr is not
available, the base attribute value is returned |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| ProcessName | A valid process name. |
| AttrName | The attribute for which you want to retrieve a value. This argument must be a valid attribute of
the process. |
| LangLocaleCode | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code for which you want to return a value. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the international language codes listed in the
}Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the user's current locale is used as the
LangLocaleCode argument. If an attribute value does not exist for the LangLocaleCode, the value for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode is returned. If an attribute value does not exist for an associated parent
LangLocaleCode, the base attribute value is returned. For example if the LangLocaleCode is fr-CA , the function returns the attribute
value for the fr-CA (French-Canada) locale if available. If the attribute value for fr-CA is not available, the function attempts to return the attribute value for the
parent fr (French) locale. If the attribute value for fr is not
available, the base attribute value is returned |

#### Example Notes

In this example, the function returns the numeric value of the Store_Code attribute of the
Daily_Sales process for the French locale.

#### Examples

```ti
ProcessAttrNL('Daily_Sales', 'Store_Code', 'fr');
```

### ProcessAttrPutN

- Category: Attribute Manipulation TurboIntegrator Functions
- Last updated: 2025-03-19
- Tags: action:update, category:attribute, feature:locale, feature:turbointegrator-only, object:attribute, object:process, value:number, value:string
- Source: https://www.ibm.com/docs/api/v1/content/SSD29G_2.0.0/com.ibm.swg.ba.cognos.tm1_ref.2.0.0.doc/r_ti_func_processattrputn.html?parsebody=true&lang=en

#### Description

ProcessAttrPutN assigns a value to a numeric process attribute.

This function is valid in TM1® TurboIntegrator processes
only.

- Valid in: turbointegrator

#### Syntax

```ti
ProcessAttrPutN(NumericValue, CubeName, AttrName, [LangLocaleCode] );
```

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| NumericValue | number | The value you want to assign to a process attribute. |
| ProcessName | string | The process for which you want to assign an attribute value. |
| AttrName | string | The attribute whose value you want to assign. |
| LangLocaleCode | string | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code to which the NumericValue applies. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the ISO 639-1 international language codes listed in
the }Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the base attribute value is updated. |

#### Arguments

| Argument | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NumericValue | The value you want to assign to a process attribute. |
| ProcessName | The process for which you want to assign an attribute value. |
| AttrName | The attribute whose value you want to assign. |
| LangLocaleCode | This optional parameter specifies the language locale code to which the NumericValue applies. Valid LangLocaleCode values correspond to the ISO 639-1 international language codes listed in
the }Cultures control dimension. When the LangLocaleCode is not specified or is omitted, the base attribute value is updated. |

#### Example Notes

This example assigns the value 8051997 to the Store_Code attribute of the Daily_Sales process for
the French language locale code.

#### Examples

```ti
ProcessAttrPutN(8051997, 'Daily_Sales', 'Store_Code','fr');
```
